- @accessDate (Input): The access date of the Depot Authorisation records to retrieve. This parameter is used in the WHERE clause for filtering the results.

**3. Full Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**

The stored procedure reads data from the following tables and their respective columns:
- TAMS_TAR (TARNo)
- TAMS_Depot_Auth (ID, AccessDate, TarID, DepotAuthStatusId, RemarkID)
- TAMS_Depot_Auth_Workflow (DTCAuthId, WorkflowID, CheckBoxValue, WFStatus, ActionOn, WorkflowID)
- TAMS_Depot_Auth_Remark (RemarkID, Remark)
- TAMS_WFStatus (ID, [Order])
- TAMS_User (LoginId, Name)

**4. Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:**

The stored procedure does not have any explicit conditional or business rules specified in the provided code. However, the order of results is determined by the ASC sorting on DepotAuthStatusId, and there may be additional business logic related to the individual tables involved.

**5. Additional Notes:**

- The stored procedure orders the results by Ascending order of DepotAuthStatusId.
- The SET NOCOUNT ON command is added at the beginning to prevent extra result sets from interfering with SELECT statements, such as message count notifications during multiple row operations.

Procedure: dbo.SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCAuthEndorser
 **Documentation for the Stored Procedure SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCAuthEndorser**

**Full Workflow and Edge Cases:**

1. This stored procedure retrieves the Depot DTCAuth Endorser information based on a provided access date and LAN ID.
2. The workflow for this stored procedure is as follows:
   - Retrieve the WorkflowID for the OCCAuth workflow type with Depot track type from the TAMS_Workflow table.
   - Retrieve the Endorser roles that are assigned to duty staff in the NEL line of the Depot tracktype on the provided access date from the TAMS_OCC_Duty_Roster and TAMS_User tables.
   - Join the TAMS_Endorser table with the retrieved roles, and only include rows where the WorkflowID matches the one obtained in step 1, the IsActive flag is set to 1, and the WFType equals DTCAuth.
   - Finally, filter the results further by ensuring that the EffectiveDate is less than or equal to the provided access date and the ExpiryDate is greater than or equal to the provided access date.
3. Edge cases:
   - If no Endorser role matches the provided LAN ID on the specified access date, an empty result set will be returned.
   - If there are multiple Endorser roles matching the conditions, only one row will be returned due to the inner join. It's recommended to implement additional query optimizations or modifications if encountering performance issues with multiple roles.

**Complete Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:**
- @accessDate (input parameter): The access date for which the Depot DTCAuth Endorser information is requested. This is a DATE data type.
- @lanid (input parameter): The LAN ID of the user requesting the Depot DTCAuth Endorser information. This is an nvarchar(50) data type.

**Full Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**
This stored procedure performs read operations on the following tables:
- TAMS_Workflow
- TAMS_Endorser
- TAMS_WFStatus
- TAMS_OCC_Duty_Roster
- TAMS_Roster_Role
- TAMS_User

It reads data from these tables to construct the result set containing Depot DTCAuth Endorser information. No write operations are performed within this stored procedure.

**All Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:**
- The stored procedure checks if the provided LAN ID is present in the TAMS_OCC_Duty_Roster for the specified access date, line (NEL), and track type (Depot). If it exists, the Access column will be set to 1, indicating that the user has access. Otherwise, the Access column will be set to 0, indicating no access.
- The stored procedure filters the results based on the EffectiveDate and ExpiryDate of each endorser role to ensure that the provided access date falls within the validity period.

**Additional Notes:**
This stored procedure assumes that the necessary foreign key relationships are established between the tables involved in the query. Also, it's essential to validate user input parameters for potential security risks or improper data inputs. Furthermore, consider implementing error handling and exception mechanisms to better handle unexpected conditions during execution.

Procedure: dbo.SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCAuthPowerzone
 Title: Stored Procedure Documentation - `SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCAuthPowerzone`

1. Workflow and Edge Cases
   - The stored procedure retrieves Depot Authorization information related to DTCAuth SPKS (Special Protection Konnection Areas) for a specific access date.
   - Edge cases:
     - If no records are found for the given access date, an empty result set will be returned.
     - In case of multiple records for the same access date, they will be ordered by AuthID and ID in ascending order.

2. Input/Output Parameter Descriptions
   - `@accessDate` (input): The specific date for which Depot Authorization SPKS information is requested. This parameter should be passed as a SQL Date type.

3. Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior
   - The stored procedure performs read operations on the following tables:
     - `TAMS_Depot_Auth`
     - `TAMS_Depot_Auth_Powerzone`
     - `TAMS_Power_Sector`
     - `TAMS_WFStatus` (only for getting Workflow ID)
     - `TAMS_User` (for retrieving user names associated with various actions)
   - The stored procedure does not perform any write operations.

4. Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects
   - Only active Power Sectors (`IsActive=1`) are considered in the query results.
   - If a record in `TAMS_Depot_Auth` has no corresponding entry in `TAMS_Depot_Auth_Powerzone`, it will still be included in the result set with NULL values for columns related to Power Sector information.

5. Complete SQL Code

```sql
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCAuthPowerzone]
    @accessDate as Date
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    SELECT * from (
        Select WFType,AuthID,PowerSector,TAMS_Power_Sector.ID,PowerOffType,PowerOffTiming,RackedOutType,RackedOutTiming,PowerOnType,PowerOnTiming,RackedInType,RackedInTiming,PowerOffActionUser.Name as PowerOffActionBy,RackOffActionUser.Name as RackedOffActionBy,PowerOnActionUser.Name as PowerOnActionBy,RackOnActionUser.Name as RackedInActionBy,StatusID,Z.ID as workflowid,TAMS_Depot_Auth_Powerzone.IsBuffer,DENSE_RANK() OVER (ORDER BY AuthID) as rowspan
        from TAMS_Depot_Auth
        LEFT JOIN TAMS_Depot_Auth_Powerzone ON TAMS_Depot_Auth.ID=TAMS_Depot_Auth_Powerzone.AuthID
        LEFT JOIN TAMS_Power_Sector ON TAMS_Depot_Auth_Powerzone.PowerzoneID=TAMS_Power_Sector.ID
        LEFT JOIN (Select * from TAMS_WFStatus where WFType='DTCAuth') Z ON Z.WFStatusId=StatusID
        LEFT JOIN TAMS_User PowerOffActionUser ON PowerOffActionUser.LoginId=PowerOffActionBy
        LEFT JOIN TAMS_User PowerOnActionUser ON PowerOnActionUser.LoginID=PowerOnActionBy
        LEFT JOIN TAMS_User RackOffActionUser ON RackOffActionUser.LoginId=RackedOffActionBy
        LEFT JOIN TAMS_User RackOnActionUser ON RackOnActionUser.LoginID=RackedInActionBy
        where TAMS_Depot_Auth.AccessDate=@accessDate and TAMS_Power_Sector.IsActive=1
    ) A
    order by A.AuthID ASC,A.ID ASC
END
GO
```

Procedure: dbo.SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCAuthSPKS
 Title: SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCAuthSPKS Stored Procedure Documentation

1. Workflow and Edge Cases:
   - This stored procedure is designed to retrieve Depot Auth DTC Auth SPKS details along with related information for a specific access date.
   - If the provided `@accessDate` does not exist in the TAMS_Depot_Auth table, the procedure will return an empty result set.
   - If there are multiple entries for the same access date, the stored procedure will return all matching records.

2. Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:
   - `@accessDate` (Input): The specific access date to retrieve Depot Auth DTC Auth SPKS details for. This parameter should be a SQL Server `date` type.

3. Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:
   - Tables interacted in this stored procedure are:
     - TAMS_Depot_Auth
     - TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS
     - TAMS_WFStatus
     - TAMS_User (for ProtectOffActionBy and ProtectOnActionBy aliases)
   - The stored procedure reads data from these tables to assemble the result set. No write operations are performed.

4. Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:
   - The WHERE clause filters the results based on the provided `@accessDate`.
   - LEFT JOINs are used for cases where matching records may or may not exist in the referenced tables.

5. Complete Query:

```sql
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCAuthSPKS]
    -- Add the parameters for the stored procedure here
    @accessDate as Date
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    Select AuthID,
           TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS.SPKSID,
           TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS.ProtectOffType,
           TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS.ProtectOffTiming,
           TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS.ProtectOnType,
           TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS.ProtectOnTiming,
           TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS.StatusID,
           ProtectOffActionBy.Name as ProtectOffActionBy,
           ProtectOnActionBy.Name as ProtectOnActionBy,
           Z.ID as workflowid
    from TAMS_Depot_Auth
         LEFT JOIN TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS ON TAMS_Depot_Auth.ID=TAMS_Depot_DTCAuth_SPKS.AuthID
         LEFT JOIN (Select * from TAMS_WFStatus where WFType='DTCAuth') Z ON Z.WFStatusId=StatusID
         LEFT JOIN TAMS_User ProtectOffActionBy ON ProtectOffActionBy.LoginId = ProtectOffActionBy
         LEFT JOIN TAMS_User ProtectOnActionBy ON ProtectOnActionBy.LoginId = ProtectOnActionBy
    where TAMS_Depot_Auth.AccessDate=@accessDate
END
GO
```

Procedure: dbo.SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCRoster
 **Stored Procedure Documentation: SP_TAMS_Depot_GetDTCRoster**

**1. Workflow and Edge Cases:**
This stored procedure is designed to retrieve a roster for Depot duties on a specific date. The workflow involves selecting distinct RosterCodes from the `TAMS_OCC_Duty_Roster` table where `tracktype` is 'depot'. Then, it performs a left outer join with the same table but filtered by the input parameter `@date` and `tracktype='depot`. Finally, it performs another left outer join with the `TAMS_User` table on the condition that the `DutyStaffId` from the joined `TAMS_OCC_Duty_Roster` matches the `Userid` of the `TAMS_User`.

Edge cases:
- If there is no data in the `TAMS_OCC_Duty_Roster` table for the specified date and 'depot' tracktype, no results will be returned.
- If a RosterCode does not have any corresponding duty staff for the specified date, the corresponding row will have NULL values for Name and LoginId columns.

**2. Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:**
- `@date`: This is an input parameter of type `Date`. It represents the target date for which the Depot roster should be retrieved.

**3. Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**
- **Read Behavior:** The stored procedure reads data from the following tables and columns:
  - TAMS_OCC_Duty_Roster (Shift, RosterCode, OperationDate, DutyStaffId)
  - TAMS_User (Name, LoginId, Userid)
- **Write Behavior:** This stored procedure does not write any data to the tables. It only reads and returns data for a specific date.

**4. Conditional/Business Rules and Side-effects:**
- The left outer join with the `TAMS_OOC_Duty_Roster` table filters the records by the 'depot' tracktype and specified date.
- The left outer join with the `TAMS_User` table is performed on the condition that the `DutyStaffId` from the joined `TAMS_OCC_Duty_Roster` matches the `Userid` of the `TAMS_User`. This allows for matching duty staff members to their respective RosterCodes.
- If a RosterCode does not have any corresponding duty staff for the specified date, the corresponding row will have NULL values for Name and LoginId columns.

**5. Side Effects:**
This stored procedure does not have any noticeable side effects as it only reads data from the tables and returns the results. It does not modify or update any data within the tables.

- `ParaValue3`: The third value of the parameter.
- `ParaTime`: The time associated with the parameter.

**Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:**

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_GetTarByTarId
 **Stored Procedure Documentation**

**Procedure Name:** `dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_GetTarByTarId`

**Purpose:** This stored procedure retrieves the details of a specific TAR (Transmission Access Request) by its ID. It also fetches related information about the Power Sector and SPKSZone the TAR belongs to, and the status of the TAR.

**Full Workflow and Edge Cases:**
1. The stored procedure accepts an integer input parameter `@TarId`. If the provided `@TarId` is 0 or not present, no result will be returned as there is no valid TAR to fetch.
2. It first retrieves PowerSector data associated with the given TAR ID by joining the `TAMS_Power_Sector` and `TAMS_TAR_Power_Sector` tables based on their respective IDs, ensuring that only active sectors are selected and the buffer flag is set to 0. The Power Sector names are concatenated and formatted using the `@PowerZone` variable.
3. If the `@PowerZone` variable contains any data after trimming, it removes the last comma (`,`) to ensure proper output formatting.
4. Next, it fetches SPKSZone data associated with the given TAR ID by joining the `TAMS_SPKSZone` and `TAMS_TAR_SPKSZone` tables based on their respective IDs, ensuring that only active zones are selected. The SPKSZone names are concatenated and formatted using the `@SPKSZone` variable.
5. If the `@SPKSZone` variable contains any data after trimming, it removes the last comma (`,`) to ensure proper output formatting.
6. It then selects all details of the TAR with the given ID from the `TAMS_TAR` table. The selected fields include TAR-related information, PowerZone, SPKSZone, and TAR status-related data such as status, withdrawal date, withdrawal by, and workflow status.
7. If multiple records have the same TAR status, it selects the record with the latest WorkType equal to 'TARWFStatus'.
8. The stored procedure returns a single result row containing all fetched details.

**Input Parameters:**
- `@TarId`: An integer representing the ID of the Transmission Access Request. It is required and has a default value of 0.

**Output Parameters:**
- None. The stored procedure returns a single result row with multiple columns containing the fetched TAR details, PowerZone, SPKSZone, and TAR status-related data.

**Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**
- `TAMS_Power_Sector`: Read operation to fetch Power Sector details.
- `TAMS_TAR_Power_Sector`: Read operation to fetch the association between TARs and Power Sectors.
- `TAMS_SPKSZone`: Read operation to fetch SPKSZone details.
- `TAMS_TAR_SPKSZone`: Read operation to fetch the association between TARs and SPKSZones.
- `TAMS_TAR`: Read operation to fetch TAR details.
- `TAMS_WFStatus`: Read operation to fetch the workflow status associated with the TAR based on its line, track type, and worktype.

**Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:**
- Only active Power Sectors and SPKSZones are selected (`IsActive = 1`).
- The buffer flag for TAR_Power_Sector is set to 0.
- If the `@PowerZone` or `@SPKSZone` variables contain a comma (`,`) at the end, it will be removed before returning the values.
- If multiple records have the same TAR status, it selects the record with the latest WorkType equal to 'TARWFStatus'.

**Side Effects:**
The stored procedure does not modify any data; it only retrieves information from various tables and formats the Power Sector and SPKSZone names.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_GetTarEnquiryResult_Department
 The stored procedure `[dbo].[sp_TAMS_Depot_GetTarEnquiryResult_Department]` is designed to retrieve TAR (Technical Appraisal Report) information based on various parameters.

**Workflow and Edge Cases:**
1. The procedure checks if the user has a specific role in the system by joining the `TAMS_User`, `TAMS_User_Role`, and `TAMS_Role` tables.
2. If the user has one of the following roles: NEL_ChiefController, NEL_DCC, NEL_ApplicantHOD, NEL_SDS, NEL_TAPApprover, NEL_TAPHOD, NEL_TAPVerifier, the `@IsAll` variable is set to 1.
3. If the user has one of the following roles: NEL_PowerEndorser or NEL_PowerHOD or NEL_PFR, the `@IsPower` variable is set to 1.
4. If the user has the role NEL_ApplicantHOD, the `@IsDep` variable is set to 1.
5. Based on these variables, the SQL query changes to filter TAR data accordingly. Users with all roles can view all TARs, Power users (PowerEndorser, PowerHOD, and PFR) can view TARs they are involved in or created by them, Applicant HOD can view only TARs under their own department.
6. The query fetches distinct companies from the `TAMS_TAR` table based on the filter conditions and sorts them with a row number.
7. Finally, the procedure executes the SQL query using dynamic SQL.

**Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:**
- `@uid AS integer = 0`: The unique identifier of the user making the request. If not provided, it defaults to 0.
- `@Line AS nvarchar(50) = NULL`: The line (NEL for NEL depot and DTLD for DTL depot) for which TARs are requested. If not provided, it is null.
- `@TrackType AS nvarchar(50) = NULL`: The type of track for which TARs are requested. If not provided, it is null.
- `@TarType AS nvarchar(50) = NULL`: The type of TAR for which enquiry is made. If not provided, it is null.
- `@AccessType AS nvarchar(50) = NULL`: The access type for which TARs are requested. If not provided, it is null.
- `@TarStatusId AS integer = 0`: The status ID of the TAR for which enquiry is made. If not provided, it defaults to 0.
- `@AccessDateFrom as nvarchar(50) = NULL`: The start date for accessing the TARs. If not provided, it is null.
- `@AccessDateTo as nvarchar(50) = NULL`: The end date for accessing the TARs. If not provided, it is null.

**Full table/column interactions and read/write behavior:**
- Reads from the `TAMS_User`, `TAMS_User_Role`, and `TAMS_Role` tables to check the user's role.
- Reads from the `TAMS_TAR` table to fetch TAR information based on filter conditions.
- Writes the result set as a row numbered output.

**Conditional/business rules and side-effects:**
- The query filters TAR data based on user roles, line, track type, tar type, access type, status ID, access date range, and line.
- The procedure uses dynamic SQL to build the final query based on user roles.
- The procedure prints the generated SQL query before executing it for debugging purposes.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_GetTarSectorsByAccessDateAndLine
 **Stored Procedure Documentation**

Title: `sp_TAMS_Depot_GetTarSectorsByAccessDateAndLine`

Author: Reno Adipura

Creation Date: 09 Feb 2021

Last Updated: 10/10/2025

**Description:**
This stored procedure retrieves TAR sectors based on the provided access date and line for Depot tracks. It also handles setting a common color code for sectors with the same Tar No and SameSector.

**Workflow:**
1. Initialization of temporary table #TMP.
2. If the @Line parameter is 'NEL', it performs the following steps:
   - Query data from TAMS_Sector, TAMS_TAR_Sector, and TAMS_TAR tables based on conditions mentioned below in the 'Conditional Rules' section. The results are inserted into the #TMP table.
3. Sets a common ColourCode for sectors with the same Tar No and SameSector by updating #TMP.
4. Selects all records from the #TMP table, orders them by [Order] in ascending order.
5. Finally, it drops the temporary table #TMP.

**Edge Cases:**
- If @Line is not 'NEL', no data will be returned.
- If no records match the provided parameters, an empty result set will be returned.

**Input Parameters:**
- `@AccessDate`: The access date for which TAR sectors are to be retrieved (date type).
- `@Line`: The line identifier for Depot tracks ('NEL' only is supported currently).

**Output Parameters:**
This stored procedure does not have any output parameters. It returns a result set with the selected records from #TMP.

**Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**
- TAMS_Sector: `id`, `Line`, `TrackType`, `IsActive`, `EffectiveDate`, `ExpiryDate` (Read)
- TAMS_TAR_Sector: `Id`, `SectorId`, `TarId`, `AccessDate`, `AccessType`, `SameSector`, `IsSpecialSector`, `Direction`, `IsBuffer`, `IsGap` (Read/Write)
- TAMS_TAR: `Id`, `ColourCode` (Read)
- #TMP: All columns are read and written during the execution of the stored procedure.

**Conditional Rules:**
- The query filters data based on the following conditions:
  - AccessDate is equal to the provided @AccessDate.
  - TARStatusId = 9.
  - AccessType is either 'Possession' or ('Protection' AND isExclusive = 1).
  - Line, TrackType, IsActive, EffectiveDate, and ExpiryDate are as per the provided conditions in TAMS_Sector.
- The query also filters data based on whether Direction is provided as a parameter or not. If it's not provided, all directions will be considered.

**Side-Effects:**
- When the stored procedure runs, it creates a temporary table and modifies its data during execution. After completing its task, the temporary table is dropped.
- The ColourCode from #TMP with SameSector not null, TarNo not null, and ColourCode not null will be set to other rows with the same conditions in #TMP. This might lead to multiple rows having the same color code if there are more than one row meeting those conditions.

 Title: Documentation for the Stored Procedure `sp_TAMS_Depot_GetTarSectorsByTarId`

   - TAMS_TAR: Read operation on column `Id`.

   - If a user exists in the `TAMS_User` table, the output parameter `@res` is set to 1, indicating that the user has access.
   - If no matching user is found in the `TAMS_User` table, the output parameter `@res` is set to 0, indicating that the user does not have access.

Procedure: dbo.SP_TAMS_Depot_GetWFStatus
 Title: Documentation for Stored Procedure [dbo].[SP_TAMS_Depot_GetWFStatus]

1. Workflow and Edge Cases:
   - The stored procedure SP_TAMS_Depot_GetWFStatus is designed to retrieve the ID and WFStatusId from the TAMS_WFStatus table where the WFType is 'DTCAuth'. There are no edge cases defined in this specific stored procedure, but it's important to note that edge cases may exist when integrating it with other parts of the application.

2. Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:
   - There are no input parameters for this stored procedure as it directly queries the database without any user-provided input. The output is a result set containing the ID and WFStatusId columns from the TAMS_WFStatus table, filtered by 'DTCAuth' WFType.

3. Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:
   - This stored procedure reads data from the TAMS_WFStatus table, specifically the ID, WFStatusId, and WFType columns. It does not perform any write operations on these tables.

4. Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:
   - There are no conditional or business rules defined in this stored procedure as it simply queries the database based on a specific filter condition. However, side-effects may occur when the result set is used by other procedures or applications.

5. Additional Notes:
   - The stored procedure is designed for retrieving Workflow Status information related to DTCAuth type. It might be integrated with other stored procedures or applications that handle TAMS Depot Inbox, specifically DTL and NEL types. It's essential to ensure proper data consistency when integrating this stored procedure with other parts of the system.

6. Usage Example:
   - To execute the stored procedure, use the following syntax:
     ```
     EXEC SP_TAMS_Depot_GetWFStatus;
     ```
     This will return a result set containing ID and WFStatusId columns for the DTCAuth type.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_Inbox_Child_OnLoad
 Title: Stored Procedure Documentation - `sp_TAMS_Depot_Inbox_Child_OnLoad`

Overview:
This stored procedure is designed to retrieve a list of TAR records from the TAMS database for a specific user, Line, TrackType, SectorID, and date range. It handles the loading of child records for the Depot Inbox, filtering by status, and ensuring that only pending workflows are included.

Full Workflow and Edge Cases:
1. The stored procedure initializes a few variables and creates temporary tables to store intermediate results.
2. The `@UserID` variable is set using the provided login user's ID from the TAMS_USER table.
3. The current date is obtained and formatted for use in queries.
4. Three temporary tables (#TmpSector, #TmpInbox, and #TmpInboxList) are created to store sector and TAR data during the execution of the stored procedure.
5. The temporary table `#TmpSector` is populated with sectors that meet the specified Line, TrackType, and date range conditions.
6. Two queries are used to construct the #TmpInbox table. The first query retrieves all pending TAR records associated with the user's sector(s), while the second query collects TAR records belonging to other sectors (not yet assigned to the user). Both queries filter by AccessDate, TARType, IsBuffer, and TrackType.
7. A cursor is utilized to process each TAR record in the #TmpInbox table. If a TAR record has not been processed by any other user, it is added to the temporary table `#TmpInboxList`. Otherwise, the ActionBy field from the TAMS_TAR_Workflow table is checked for the current user's ID.
8. The final result set contains the TAR records that belong to the specified SectorID from the #TmpInboxList temporary table.
9. After processing all records, the temporary tables are dropped.

Input Parameters:
1. `@Line` (NVARCHAR(10)) - Line for the sector of interest
2. `@TrackType` (NVARCHAR(50)) - Track type for the sector of interest
3. `@AccessDate` (NVARCHAR(20)) - Access date filter, optional
4. `@TARType` (NVARCHAR(20)) - TAR type filter, optional
5. `@LoginUser` (NVARCHAR(50)) - Login user for the current session
6. `@SectorID` (INT) - Sector ID to filter the final result set

Output Parameters:
None

Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:
- TAMS_USER: Read only, used to get UserID based on LoginId
- TAMS_Sector: Read only, used to populate #TmpSector table
- TAMS_TAR, TAMS_Sector, TAMS_TAR_Sector, TAMS_TAR_Workflow, TAMS_Endorser: Read only, used to construct the #TmpInbox and #TAMS_InboxList tables
- #TmpSector, #TmpInbox, #TmpInboxList: Write only, used for intermediate storage during execution

Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:
- Only pending workflows (WFStatus like '%Pending%') are included in the result set.
- The IsBuffer column from TAMS_Sector is filtered to exclude buffer sectors.
- For each sector, TAR records are checked for processing by other users before adding them to the final result set. This ensures that duplicate assignments are avoided.

Limitations and Assumptions:
- The stored procedure assumes that all date comparisons are done using the specified format (103).
- The cursor implementation may not be the most efficient approach for large datasets, but it is used here to handle complex business rules.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_Inbox_Master_OnLoad
 Title: Documentation for the stored procedure `[dbo].[sp_TAMS_Depot_Inbox_Master_OnLoad]`

1. Workflow and Edge Cases:
   The stored procedure `sp_TAMS_Depot_Inbox_Master_OnLoad` is designed to retrieve a list of pending TARs (Transportation Access Requests) based on specific filter conditions for a given user, line, track type, access date, and TAR type. It also handles the case where a user has already acknowledged the same TAR by checking the WorkflowStatus in `TAMS_TAR_Workflow`. If the WorkflowStatus is not 'Pending', it checks if the ActionBy field matches the logged-in user's ID, and if not, it adds the TAR to the list of pending TARs for that user.

2. Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:
   - `@Line` (NVARCHAR(10)): The line for which the TARs are to be retrieved. It can be NULL.
   - `@TrackType` (NVARCHAR(50)): The track type for which the TARs are to be retrieved. It can be NULL.
   - `@AccessDate` (NVARCHAR(20)): The access date for the TARs. It can be NULL, in which case all TARs are returned.
   - `@TARType` (NVARCHAR(20)): The type of TAR to be retrieved. It can be NULL, in which case all TAR types are considered.
   - `@LoginUser` (NVARCHAR(50)): The ID of the user for whom the pending TARs are to be retrieved.

3. Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:
   This stored procedure interacts with several tables in the database, mainly `TAMS_USER`, `TAMS_Sector`, `TAMS_TAR`, `TAMS_TAR_Sector`, `TAMS_TAR_Workflow`, and `TAMS_Endorser`. It reads data from these tables to construct the temporary tables `#TmpSector`, `#TmpInbox`, and `#TmpInboxList` and writes data into them. Finally, it selects data from the temporary table `#TmpSector` for output.

4. Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:
   - The stored procedure filters TARs based on the specified line, track type, access date, and TAR type.
   - It only considers active sectors that fall within the effective and expiry dates.
   - It checks if the TAR is a buffer or not (i.e., `IsBuffer = 0`).
   - It ensures that the user has the appropriate role for endorsing the TAR.
   - If a TAR's WorkflowStatus is not 'Pending', it checks if the ActionBy field matches the logged-in user's ID. If not, it adds the TAR to the list of pending TARs for that user.

5. Cursor Usage:
   The stored procedure uses two cursors: `@Cur01` and `@Cur02`. `@Cur01` is used to iterate through the pending TARs, while `@Cur02` is used to check if a specific user has already acknowledged a particular TAR.

6. Example Usage:
   To execute this stored procedure, use the following syntax:

```sql
EXEC [dbo].[sp_TAMS_Depot_Inbox_Master_OnLoad] 'DTL', '', '', 'CSAPEX57';
EXEC [dbo].[sp_TAMS_Depot_Inbox_Master_OnLoad] 'NEL', '', '', 'CSAPEX57';
```

The above examples retrieve the pending TARs for lines DTL and NEL, respectively, for user 'CSAPEX57'.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_AckSurrender
 **Stored Procedure Documentation**

Title: `sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_AckSurrender`

**Workflow and Edge Cases:**

1. The stored procedure is designed to acknowledge the surrender of a Transport Asset Request (TAR) in the Transport Asset Management System (TAMS).
2. It first checks if the TAR already has a TOA status of 4, indicating it is available for surrender. If not, an error message is returned.
3. If the TAR is eligible for surrender, it updates the TOA status to 5, sets the AckSurrenderTime and UpdatedOn fields with the current date and time, and sets the UpdatedBy field to the provided user ID.
4. The procedure then inserts a new row in `TAMS_TOA_Audit` with details of the surrendered TOA.
5. Next, it checks if all TARs on the same line as the surrendered one have been surrendered (TOA status 5). If not, an error message is returned.
6. For lines belonging to NEL DCC, if all TARs have been surrendered, it initiates the second phase of the Operational Control Centre (OCC) by updating the depot authentication workflow and status.
7. After these operations, it sends an SMS notification to the mobile number associated with the surrendered TOA, notifying them that their surrender has been acknowledged.
8. If any error occurs during the execution of the stored procedure, it rolls back the transaction and returns an error message.

**Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:**

- `@TARID` (BIGINT): The unique identifier of the Transport Asset Request to be surrendered.
- `@UserID` (NVARCHAR(500)): The user ID of the individual performing the surrender.
- `@Message` (NVARCHAR(500), output): A message containing the status of the operation, which is returned as an output parameter.

**Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**

- `TAMS_User`: Reads the user ID associated with the provided login ID.
- `TAMS_TAR`: Reads the details of the Transport Asset Request to be surrendered.
- `TAMS_TOA`: Updates the TOA status, AckSurrenderTime, UpdatedOn, and UpdatedBy fields for the surrendered TOA; inserts a new row in the `TAMS_TOA_Audit` table with details of the surrendered TOA.
- `TAMS_Depot_Auth`: Updates the depot authentication status and workflow if the TAR belongs to NEL DCC and all other TARs on the same line have been surrendered.

**Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:**

1. The stored procedure performs a series of checks to ensure that only eligible Transport Asset Requests can be surrendered. If an ineligible request is attempted to be surrendered, an error message is returned.
2. If all TARs on the same line as the surrendered one have not been surrendered, an error message is returned.
3. For NEL DCC lines, if all TARs have been surrendered, the stored procedure initiates the second phase of the OCC by updating the depot authentication workflow and status.
4. An SMS notification is sent to the mobile number associated with the surrendered TOA upon successful surrender acknowledgement.
5. If any error occurs during the execution of the stored procedure, the transaction is rolled back, and an error message is returned.

**Side-Effects:**

1. Updates to `TAMS_TOA` and `TAMS_TOA_Audit` tables.
2. Updates to `TAMS_Depot_Auth` table if the TAR belongs to NEL DCC and all other TARs on the same line have been surrendered.
3. SMS notifications are sent upon successful surrender acknowledgement.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_GrantTOA
 **Stored Procedure Documentation:**

Title: `sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_GrantTOA`

Description: This stored procedure is designed to grant a Time Out Authorization (TOA) for a Trip Authorization Request (TAR). It checks the TOA status, generates a unique reference number, updates the TOA status and related audit information, sends an SMS to the user, and logs any errors that occur during the process.

**Full Workflow:**

1. The procedure starts by initializing an internal transaction and checking if there is already an ongoing transaction. If not, it begins a new one.
2. It sets the output message variable to an empty string.
3. It declares several local variables for storing TAR-related data (TARNo, Line, OPDate, AccessType, Site, HPNo, and TOAStatus) as well as a SMS message variable.
4. It retrieves the TAR data based on the provided TARID and checks if the TOA status is 2 (grantable). If the TOA status is 2, it proceeds to generate a reference number, update the TOA status and related audit information, send an SMS to the user, and log any errors that occur during the process.
5. If the TOA status is not 2 or an error occurs during the process, it sets the output message with an appropriate error message and rolls back the transaction if necessary.
6. If there are no errors, the transaction is committed and the output message contains a success message.

**Edge Cases:**

1. If the provided TARID does not correspond to a valid TAR or if there's an issue retrieving TAR data, the procedure will set the output message with an appropriate error message (e.g., 'Invalid TAR status. Please refresh RGS.').
2. If the TOA has already been granted (TOAStatus = 3), the procedure will set the output message with an appropriate error message (e.g., '1' - TOA already granted. Please refresh RGS.).
3. If there's an issue sending the SMS to the user, the procedure will set the output message with an appropriate error message (e.g., 'Error SMS Sending').

**Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:**

- `@TARID`: The unique identifier of the Trip Authorization Request for which a TOA is being granted. (BIGINT, default value 0)
- `@EncTARID`: An encrypted version of the Trip Authorization Request ID. (NVARCHAR(250), optional output parameter)
- `@UserID`: The ID of the user who is granting the TOA. (NVARCHAR(500))
- `@toacallbacktiming`: The callback time for the granted TOA. (datetime, optional input parameter)
- `@Message`: A message that contains an error or success status. (NVARCHAR(500), optional output parameter)

**Full Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**

This stored procedure interacts with the following tables and performs read and write operations:

- `TAMS_TAR`: Reads data related to a Trip Authorization Request. Writes data if there's an error during the process.
- `TAMS_TOA`: Reads and writes data related to Time Out Authorizations, including granting a TOA and updating its status, TOA number, callback time, and audit information.
- `TAMS_TOA_Audit`: Writes data for the Trip Authorization Request audit trail when a TOA is granted.

**Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:**

1. If the TOA status is 2 (grantable), it generates a reference number, updates the TOA status and related audit information, sends an SMS to the user, and logs any errors that occur during the process.
2. If there's an error during the process or an issue sending the SMS to the user, it sets the output message with an appropriate error message (e.g., 'Invalid TAR status. Please refresh RGS.', 'Error SMS Sending') and rolls back the transaction if necessary.
3. If there are no errors, the transaction is committed and the output message contains a success message.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_OnLoad
 **Stored Procedure Documentation: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_OnLoad**

This stored procedure is designed to retrieve data for the Rail Grid System (RGS) screen, specifically for depot access requests. The procedure fetches relevant information such as TAR number, electrical sections, power off time, circuit break out time, parties involved, contact numbers, remarks, TOA status, IsTOAAuth, color code, grant TOA enable status, update QTS time, access type, and other related details.

**Full Workflow and Edge Cases:**
1. The stored procedure accepts three input parameters: `@Line`, `@TrackType`, and `@accessDate`. These parameters are used to filter the data returned by the query.
   - `@Line`: The line of the rail grid system (e.g., NEL, DTL). If not provided, it defaults to NULL.
   - `@TrackType`: The type of track being accessed. If not provided, it defaults to NULL.
   - `@accessDate`: The date for which depot access requests need to be fetched. It is used to filter the data returned by the query.

2. The procedure first sets up variables for RGS possession, protection, and cancellation background values based on the line parameter and TAMS_Parameters table.

3. It then defines a time cut-off at 6 AM to determine if the operation date should be set as yesterday or today.

4. The main query is executed, which fetches data from the TAMS_TAR and TAMS_TOA tables based on the provided input parameters and conditions. The data includes:
   - Row number (Sno)
   - TARNo (unique identifier for each access request)
   - Electrical Sections (obtained using the TAMS_Get_ES_NoBufferZone function)
   - Power off time (the latest power-off timing for the specified access request and authorization, if completed)
   - Circuit break out time (the latest racking-out timing for the specified access request and authorization, if completed)
   - Parties involved in the access request (obtained using the dbo.TAMS_Get_TOA_Parties function)
   - Contact information (mobile number and tetra radio number) for parties involved
   - TOANo (TOA number, if provided)
   - CallBackTime (the time at which a callback should be made)
   - RadioMsgTime (the time the radio message was sent)
   - LineClearMsgTime (the time the line clear message was acknowledged)
   - Remarks (comments related to the access request, obtained using the SP_TAMS_RGS_Comments function)
   - TOA status (status of the TOA registration: 0 - Draft, 1 - Registered, 2 - Acknowledged Register, 3 - TOA Granted, 4 - Surrender, 5 - Acknowledge Surrender, 6 - Cancel)
   - IsTOAAuth (indicates if the occ authorization for the access request is complete)
   - Color code (based on the TOA status and background values for possession, protection, and cancellation)
   - Grant TOA enable status (determines whether the grant TOA button should be enabled or not based on various conditions)
   - UpdQTSTime (the time the QTS was last updated)
   - AccessType (type of access: Possession, Protection, Cancellation)
   - AckGrantTOATime (time the TOA grant was acknowledged)
   - AckProtLimitTIme (time the protection limit acknowledgment was made)
   - TARID and TOAID (IDs of the access request and TOA registration, respectively)
   - InChargeNRIC (the NRIC number of the person in charge)

5. The stored procedure also includes a subquery to fetch data for cancelled requests.

6. Finally, it displays the operation date and access date for convenience.

**Business Rules and Side-Effects:**
- The stored procedure retrieves data from various tables (TAMS_TAR, TAMS_TOA, TAMS_Parameters, TAMS_Depot_Auth, and TAMS_Access_Requirement) to populate the RGS screen.
- The grant TOA enable status is determined based on multiple conditions, including the access type, TOA status, and presence of certain requirements in the Access Requirements table.
- The color code for each row is determined based on the TOA status and background values for possession, protection, and cancellation.
- If the `@Line` or `@TrackType` parameters are not provided, the procedure will use default NULL values.
- If the operation date needs to be set as yesterday (i.e., before 6 AM), it is calculated by subtracting one day from the current date. Otherwise, the current date is used.
- The main query orders the results first by access type and then by TAR number, ensuring that the data is presented in an organized manner.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_OnLoad_Enq
 Title: Documentation for Stored Procedure `dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_OnLoad_Enq`

## Workflow and Edge Cases

The stored procedure `sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_OnLoad_Enq` is designed to retrieve data related to Track Access Requests (TAR) for a given line, track type, and access date. The data includes electrical sections, power-off time, circuit breakout time, parties names, contact numbers, TOA status, color code, grant TOA enable status, update QTS time, TAR ID, TOA ID, incharge NRIC, and various timestamps.

Edge cases:
1. If the input parameters `@Line`, `@TrackType`, or `@accessDate` are null or not provided, the stored procedure will return an empty result set.
2. If there is no matching TAR record found for the provided line, track type, and access date, the stored procedure will also return an empty result set.
3. In case of any errors during execution, the stored procedure may throw exceptions that need to be handled appropriately.

## Input/Output Parameter Descriptions

- `@Line` (NVARCHAR(20)): The line for which TAR data is requested. Default value is NULL.
- `@TrackType` (nvarchar(50)): The track type associated with the TAR. Default value is null.
- `@accessDate` (Date): The access date for the TAR. Default value is NULL.

## Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior

The stored procedure interacts with several tables, including `TAMS_Parameters`, `TAMS_Depot_Auth`, `TAMS_Depot_Auth_Powerzone`, `TAMS_TAR_AccessReq`, `TAMS_Access_Requirement`, `TAMS_TAR`, and `TAMS_TOA`. It reads data from these tables and performs calculations to generate the final output.

## Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects

1. The stored procedure calculates power-off time and circuit breakout time based on the maximum power-off timing and racked out timing for the given TAR ID, access date, and operation date (which is set to the current date by default).
2. It sets the operation date to the current date minus one day when initially declared, but it can be overridden by setting `@OperationDate` during the execution of the stored procedure.
3. The stored procedure uses a user-defined function `dbo.TAMS_Get_ES_NoBufferZone()`, `dbo.TAMS_Get_TOA_Parties()`, and `dbo.SP_TAMS_RGS_Comments()` to retrieve additional data related to electrical sections, parties names, and comments respectively.
4. The stored procedure also checks if a TAR has been authorized with a status greater than or equal to 8 and returns the corresponding IsTOAAuth value.
5. The stored procedure uses conditional logic to set color codes based on TOA status and access type.
6. It sets `@TOACallBackTime` to '18:00' by default, indicating the time for TOA callback. This can be overridden if necessary during execution.
7. The stored procedure does not perform any write operations; it only reads data from the specified tables and generates the final output.

## Side-Effects

The stored procedure does not have any significant side-effects, as it only retrieves data without modifying the underlying tables. However, it may consume database resources during execution, depending on the complexity of the query and the amount of data being retrieved.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_Update_Details
 Title: Stored Procedure Documentation - `sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_Update_Details`

Overview:
This stored procedure updates the details of a TAR (Train Access Request) record, including Incharge's NRIC, Mobile Number, Tetra Radio Number, and associated Quality and Training statuses. The procedure also handles new Incharges and updates existing ones.

Workflow and Edge Cases:
1. Begin the transaction internally if it hasn't already been started.
2. Create a temporary table `#tmpnric` to store intermediate results during the execution of the stored procedure.
3. Retrieve the Line, Access Date, TOA ID, and Access Type from the TAMS_TOA and TAMS_TAR tables based on the provided TARID.
4. Query the `TAMS_Parameters` table to get the required Qualification Codes (QTSQualCode & QTSQualCodeProt) for the given Line, TrackType, and Access Date. If multiple qualifications are available, they will be stored in a comma-separated list.
5. Loop through each Qualification Code in the list, calling the appropriate sp_TAMS_Depot_TOA_QTS_Chk or sp_TAMS_TOA_QTS_Chk stored procedure to validate the Incharge's qualifications for that specific code. The results are stored in the `#tmpnric` temporary table.
6. Check if any valid qualification exists for the Incharge. If not, and the Access Type is 'Protection', the stored procedure will attempt to find a valid qualification from QTSQualCodeProt (which contains Protected Qualifications).
7. If no valid qualifications are found, the Message parameter is set to '1' indicating an Invalid Qualification status. Otherwise, the Message parameter is set to '0' indicating an Updated status.
8. Check if a new Incharge needs to be added (i.e., there is no existing Incharge with the provided NRIC). If so, the procedure will perform the following operations:
   - Delete all existing TOA_Parties records where IsInCharge = 1 for the given TARID.
   - Insert a new record into TAMS_TOA_Parties with the Incharge's details and IsInCharge set to 1.
   - Audit the changes by inserting records into TAMS_TOA_Audit, TAMS_TOA_Parties_Audit, and updating the corresponding tables.
9. If an existing Incharge exists with the provided NRIC, the procedure will only update their details (Mobile Number, Tetra Radio Number, and Auditing information).
10. Handle any errors that may occur during execution by rolling back the transaction if necessary and returning an error message.

Parameters:
- `@TARID` - The Train Access Request ID to be updated.
- `@InchargeNRIC` - The National Registration Identity Card (NRIC) number of the Incharge.
- `@MobileNo` - The Mobile Number of the Incharge.
- `@TetraRadioNo` - The Tetra Radio Number of the Incharge.
- `@UserID` - The User ID of the person performing the update operation.

Return:
The stored procedure returns a message indicating either '0' (Updated) or '1' (Invalid Qualification). It may also return an error message if an error occurs during execution.

Example Usage:
```sql
DECLARE @Message NVARCHAR(500);
EXEC sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_Update_Details @TARID, @InchargeNRIC, @MobileNo, @TetraRadioNo, @UserID, @Message OUTPUT;
SELECT @Message;
```

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_Update_Details20250403
 Title: Documentation for the stored procedure `sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_Update_Details20250403`

## Workflow and Edge Cases

The `sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_Update_Details20250403` stored procedure updates the details of a Depot or Mainline train access (TOA) record, checks the qualifications of the Incharge, and performs necessary audits. The procedure is designed to handle multiple qualifications for the Incharge and different access types (Mainline or Depot).

Edge cases include when the Incharge does not have a valid qualification, when an Incharge with the same NRIC already exists, and when there are errors during data manipulation.

## Input/Output Parameter Descriptions

1. `@TARID` (BIGINT): The Train Access Record ID for which details are to be updated.
2. `@InchargeNRIC` (NVARCHAR(50)): The National Registration Identity Card (NRIC) number of the Incharge.
3. `@MobileNo` (NVARCHAR(20)): The mobile number of the Incharge.
4. `@TetraRadioNo` (NVARCHAR(50)): The Tetra radio number of the Incharge.
5. `@UserID` (NVARCHAR(500)): The user ID of the person executing the stored procedure.
6. `@TrackType` (NVARCHAR(50), default 'Mainline'): The type of access, either Mainline or Depot.
7. `@Message` (NVARCHAR(500), output): A message indicating the outcome of the operation, either "Updated" or "Invalid Qualification".

## Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior

- `TAMS_TOA`: This table contains the main TOA data. The procedure reads from and writes to this table.
- `TAMS_TAR`: This table contains the Train Access Record data. The procedure reads from this table.
- `TAMS_Parameters`: This table stores various parameters for qualifications. The procedure reads from this table.
- `TAMS_TOA_Audit`: This table stores audit data for TOA updates. The procedure writes to this table.
- `TAMS_TOA_Parties_Audit`: This table stores audit data for TOA parties (Incharge and witnesses). The procedure writes to this table.
- `TAMS_TOA_Parties`: This table stores information about the Incharge, witnesses, and other parties involved in a TOA. The procedure reads from and writes to this table.
- `#tmpnric` (temporary table): This temporary table is created during the execution of the stored procedure to store qualification data for the Incharge. The procedure writes to and drops this table.

## Notes

- The stored procedure uses the `EncryptString` and `DecryptString` functions to secure sensitive data such as NRIC numbers.
- The stored procedure performs audits when an Incharge is added, updated, or deleted by creating corresponding entries in `TAMS_TOA_Audit` and `TAMS_TOA_Parties_Audit`.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_RGS_Update_QTS
 This is a SQL stored procedure named `SP_TAMS_Depot_SaveDTCAuthComments`. It appears to be used for saving authorization comments in the TAMS (Train Assignment and Movement System) Depot system. The comments are associated with a specific access request identified by the `TARID` parameter.

The procedure begins by checking if the user has provided an intrinsic transaction (`@IntrnlTrans`). If it is 1, the procedure will begin within a transaction. After that, it sets default values for various variables, including error handling and message return values.

Next, it starts a loop to insert comments into the `TAMS_Depot_Auth_Comments` table. The loop iterates through each comment provided in the `@Comment` parameter array. For each comment, it performs an INSERT statement with the relevant data: `TARID`, user ID (encrypted), comment, and timestamp.

After inserting all comments, the procedure checks if there were any errors during the operation. If no errors occurred, it commits the transaction (if one was started) and returns a message indicating success. If an error did occur, it rolls back the transaction, logs the error in the `TAMS_QTS_Error_Log` table, and returns a message indicating failure.

Finally, the procedure ends with FORCE_EXIT_PROC and TRAP_ERROR handlers to handle any exceptions that might have occurred during the execution of the stored procedure.

Procedure: dbo.SP_TAMS_Depot_SaveDTCAuthComments
 **Stored Procedure Documentation: SP_TAMS_Depot_SaveDTCAuthComments**

This stored procedure is designed to save comments related to Depot Authorization in the TAMS database.

**Full Workflow and Edge Cases:**

1. The procedure accepts an XML type parameter `@str` containing multiple authid-comments pairs, each representing a comment associated with a specific authorization ID.
2. A cursor is declared to iterate through the XML and insert or update comments in the TAMS_Depot_Auth_Remark table. If a RemarkID exists for the given authid, an existing remark will be updated; otherwise, a new remark will be inserted along with updating the corresponding RemarkID in the TAMS_Depot_Auth table.
3. In case of any errors during the execution, the transaction will be rolled back, and the `@success` output parameter will be set to 0.
4. If the execution is successful, the transaction will be committed, and the `@success` output parameter will be set to 1.
5. If no errors occur and no internal transactions are active, a new internal transaction will be started.

**Complete Input/Output Parameter Descriptions:**

- `@str` (readonly): XML type parameter containing multiple authid-comments pairs.
- `@success` (bit=NULL OUTPUT): Indicates whether the operation was successful or not. If 1, success; if 0, an error occurred.
- `@Message` (NVARCHAR(500) = NULL OUTPUT): A message detailing any errors that might have occurred during the execution of the stored procedure.

**Full Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**

- `TAMS_Depot_Auth`: Contains authorization records, with each record having an associated RemarkID (if a comment exists).
- `TAMS_Depot_Auth_Remark`: Stores the actual comments for each authorization.
- This procedure reads from the input XML parameter `@str`, and writes to both `TAMS_Depot_Auth_Remark` and `TAMS_Depot_Auth` tables.

**All Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:**

- If a RemarkID already exists for an authid, the existing remark will be updated instead of inserting a new one.
- In case of any errors during the execution, the transaction will be rolled back, potentially leaving the database in an inconsistent state if other processes are still accessing it.
- The stored procedure modifies data in two tables (`TAMS_Depot_Auth_Remark` and `TAMS_Depot_Auth`), which may have side effects on other parts of the application that depend on these tables. It's important to consider these potential impacts when using this stored procedure.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_SectorBooking_OnLoad
 Title: Stored Procedure Documentation - [dbo].[sp_TAMS_Depot_SectorBooking_OnLoad]

1. Workflow and Edge Cases

The stored procedure `sp_TAMS_Depot_SectorBooking_OnLoad` is designed to retrieve and populate a temporary table with sector information based on the provided input parameters. The following edge cases are considered:

   - If the provided line, track type, access date, TAR type, or access type is null or empty, the procedure will return an empty result set.
   - If there are no sectors available for the given parameters, the temporary table will remain empty.
   - If multiple sectors share the same power zone and SPKS zone, they will be combined into a single row in the output with their respective order numbers maintained.

2. Input/Output Parameter Descriptions

   - `@Line` (NVARCHAR(10)): Depot line (e.g., 'NEL' or 'DTL').
   - `@TrackType` (NVARCHAR(50)): Track type for the sector (e.g., 'Up', 'Down', 'Bi-directional').
   - `@AccessDate` (NVARCHAR(20)): Access date in the format YYYY-MM-DD.
   - `@TARType` (NVARCHAR(20)): Type of TAR (e.g., '1' or '2').
   - `@AccessType` (NVARCHAR(20)): Access type for the TAR ('Protection' or 'Possession').

3. Full Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior

The stored procedure interacts with the following tables:

   - `TAMS_Sector`: Read-only to retrieve sector data.
   - `TAMS_SPKSZone`, `TAMS_Track_SPKSZone`: Read-only to get SPKS zones for each sector.
   - `TAMS_Power_Sector`, `TAMS_Track_Power_Sector`: Read-only to get power sectors for each sector.
   - `TAMS_TAR`, `TAMS_TAR_Sector`: Read-only to determine color codes and access types for each sector based on the provided TAR type and access date.
   - `TAMS_Access_Requirement`: Read-only to retrieve operation requirements based on the provided line, track type, and whether power is required.

It reads data from these tables into a temporary table called `#ListES`, which it creates, populates, and ultimately returns as the output of the stored procedure. The `#ListES` table contains the following columns:

   - `Line` (NVARCHAR(10)): Depot line.
   - `SectorID` (BIGINT): Sector ID.
   - `Sector` (NVARCHAR(50)): Sector name.
   - `PowerZone` (NVARCHAR(100)): Power zone for the sector.
   - `SPKSZone` (NVARCHAR(100)): SPKS zone for the sector.
   - `FromTrack` (NVARCHAR(200)): Starting track for the sector.
   - `ToTrack` (NVARCHAR(200)): Ending track for the sector.
   - `IsSelected` (BIT): Whether the sector is selected or not.
   - `IsEnabled` (BIT): Whether the sector is enabled or disabled.
   - `ColorCode` (NVARCHAR(50)): Color code for the sector based on TAR data.
   - `OrderID` (INT): Sector order number.

4. Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects

The stored procedure has several conditional rules that determine whether a sector is enabled, its color code, and whether it needs to be selected or not:

   - If there's no matching TAR for the provided parameters, the sector will be enabled by default.
   - If a TAR is found with an exclusive status and the correct line, track type, and access date, it will determine the color code and whether the sector should be selected or not based on the provided TARType and AccessType.
   - If there's no matching TAR but the TARType is '2' or '3' and the AccessType is 'Protection', the sector will be enabled by default, even if it has a non-exclusive TAR.
   - If the sector already has a color code, its IsEnabled status will not change unless it meets the above conditions for a new color code.
   - If there's no matching requirement for power operation in the `TAMS_Access_Requirement` table, no side effects are applied to the sectors in the output. However, if there is a match, the stored procedure will return the OperationRequirement ID and name as the last result set.

5. Example Usage

The stored procedure can be executed using the following syntax:

```sql
EXEC sp_TAMS_Depot_SectorBooking_OnLoad 'DTL', '01/02/2021', '2', 'Protection'
```

This will return the sectors for Depot line 'DTL', TAR type '2', and access type 'Protection' on 01/02/2021, along with their respective power zones, SPKS zones, order numbers, enabled status, color codes, and track information. If there's a matching operation requirement for power, the stored procedure will also return it as an additional result set.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_SectorBooking_QTS_Chk
 **Stored Procedure Documentation**

Title: sp_TAMS_Depot_SectorBooking_QTS_Chk

Description: This stored procedure checks the qualification status of a specific individual for Depot Sector Booking QTS. It retrieves the necessary data from the QTS database and checks if the individual's qualification is valid based on the provided NRIC, Qualification Date, Line, and Track Type.

**Full Workflow**

1. The stored procedure initializes variables for message, EP Ctr, BLC Ctr, RTC Ctr, RetVal, and temporary table IDs.
2. It creates three temporary tables: #tmpqtsqc, #tmpnric, and #tmpqualcode.
3. The stored procedure truncates the temporary tables to clear any existing data.
4. It inserts the provided NRIC, Qualification Date, Line, and Track Type into the #tmpnric table.
5. A cursor is declared to iterate through the records in the #tmpnric table.
6. For each record, it retrieves the name of the individual associated with the NRIC from the QTS_Personnel table using the decrypted access ID.
7. It then queries the QTS database to find the qualifications that match the provided line and qualification date, and also meets certain conditions such as not being EPIC, OSM, TTP, or having a qualification access period of 99. The query also filters for qualifications with codes found in the #tmpqualcode table.
8. The number of qualifications found is stored in @QualCtr. If no qualifications are found (i.e., @QualCtr = 0), the status of the individual's qualification is marked as "InValid" and their name is updated in the #tmpnric table.
9. If one or more qualifications are found, the stored procedure checks if any have a suspension information. If not (i.e., @QualCtr > 0 and all records have NULL suspened_till), it then checks if the qualification date is valid based on the qualification's valid access date and valid till date.
   - If the qualification date is valid, the status of the individual's qualification is marked as "Valid" and their name is updated in the #tmpnric table.
   - If the qualification date is not valid, the status of the individual's qualification is marked as "InValid" and their name is updated in the #tmpnric table.
10. If any qualifications have suspension information, the stored procedure sets the status of the individual's qualification as "InValid" and their name is updated in the #tmpnric table.
11. The temporary tables are dropped at the end of the stored procedure.

**Edge Cases**

- If the provided NRIC, Qualification Date, Line, or Track Type are null or empty, the stored procedure will not return any results.
- If there is no qualification found for the provided NRIC, Qualification Date, Line, and Track Type, the status of the individual's qualification will be marked as "InValid".
- If the provided qualification date is invalid (i.e., it is before the valid access date or after the valid till date), the status of the individual's qualification will be marked as "InValid".
- If there are multiple qualifications found for the provided NRIC, Qualification Date, Line, and Track Type, only the most recent qualification with a NULL suspened_till will be considered.
- If any qualifications have suspension information, the status of the individual's qualification will be marked as "InValid".

**Input/Output Parameter Descriptions**

- @nric (NVARCHAR(MAX)): The National Registration Identity Card number of the individual whose qualification is to be checked.
- @qualdate (NVARCHAR(MAX)): The qualification date for which the status is to be checked.
- @line (NVARCHAR(MAX)): The line associated with the qualification.
- @TrackType (NVARCHAR(50)): The type of track (e.g., DTL).

**Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior**

The stored procedure reads from and writes to the following tables:

1. TAMS_Parameters: Retrieves the qualification code for the provided line and Track Type.
2. QTS_Personnel: Retrieves the name of the individual associated with the NRIC using the decrypted access ID.
3. QTS_Qualification: Queries the qualifications that match the provided line, qualification date, and other conditions.
4. #tmpqtsqc (temporary table): Stores the qualifications found during the query of the QTS_Qualification table.
5. #tmpnric (temporary table): Stores the NRIC, Qualification Date, Line, Track Type, name, and status of each individual.
6. #tmpqualcode (temporary table): Stores the qualification codes for the provided line and Track Type.

**Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects**

The stored procedure follows the following business rules:

1. The qualification status is marked as "Valid" if the qualification date is valid based on the qualification's valid access date and valid till date, and there are no suspension information.
2. The qualification status is marked as "InValid" in the following cases:
   - If there is no qualification found for the provided NRIC, Qualification Date, Line, and Track Type.
   - If the provided qualification date is invalid (i.e., it is before the valid access date or after the valid till date).
   - If any qualifications have suspension information.
3. The temporary tables are dropped at the end of the stored procedure.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_TOA_QTS_Chk
 **Stored Procedure Documentation**

**Procedure Name:** `dbo.sp_TAMS_Depot_TOA_QTS_Chk`

**Purpose:** This stored procedure checks the qualification status of a personnel for a specific date, line, and qualification code in the QTSDB database. It retrieves and processes the necessary data from the `QTS_Personnel`, `QTS_Qualification`, and `QTS_Personnel_Qualification` tables.

**Full Workflow and Edge Cases:**
1. The stored procedure initializes variables and sets default values for error messages, counter variables, and return values.
2. It creates a temporary table (#tmpqtsqc) to store the personnel's qualifications.
3. The temporary table is truncated before populating it with the necessary data from the `QTS_Personnel`, `QTS_Qualification`, and `QTS_Personnel_Qualification` tables, based on the provided parameters (nric, qualdate, line, QualCode).
4. The stored procedure counts the number of records in the temporary table for the given nric. If no records are found, it sets the qualification status to 'InValid'.
5. If at least one record is found, it retrieves the last access date, valid access date, valid till date, and suspension dates from the temporary table.
6. If there's a non-empty suspension_till date, the qualification status is set to 'InValid'.
7. If the provided qualdate is between the valid access date and valid till date (excluding), the qualification status is set to 'Valid'. Otherwise, it sets the qualification status to 'InValid'.
8. The stored procedure outputs the nric, name, line, qualdate, qualcode, and qualstatus.
9. Finally, the temporary table is dropped.

**Input Parameters:**
- @nric: The National Registration Identity Card (NRIC) number of the personnel to check.
- @qualdate: The date for which the qualification status is being checked. This parameter should be in the format 'YYYY-MM-DD'.
- @line: The line associated with the personnel's qualification.
- @QualCode: A comma-separated list of qualification codes to filter the results.

**Output Parameters:**
- @Message: A string message indicating whether there was an error or success in executing the stored procedure. This parameter is not explicitly outputted but may be accessed through a caller (e.g., SELECT @Message).
- @RetVal: A string return value that indicates whether the qualification status is 'Valid' or 'InValid'. This parameter is not explicitly outputted but may be accessed through a caller (e.g., SELECT @RetVal).

**Table/Column Interactions and Read/Write Behavior:**
- Temporary table `#tmpqtsqc` is created, populated, read from, and then dropped within the stored procedure.
- The following tables are queried for data: `QTS_Personnel`, `QTS_Qualification`, and `QTS_Personnel_Qualification`. No writes occur in this stored procedure on these tables.

**Conditional/Business Rules and Side-Effects:**
- If the personnel's qualification is suspended, the qualification status will be 'InValid'.
- If the provided qualdate is not between the valid access date and valid till date (excluding), the qualification status will be 'InValid'.

**Edge Cases:**
- The stored procedure handles cases where the provided nric, qualdate, line, or QualCode are NULL or empty.
- If there's no record found for the given nric in the temporary table (#tmpqtsqc), it sets the qualification status to 'InValid'.
- If the suspension_till date is not empty, the qualification status will be checked against it. Otherwise, the qualification status will be determined based on the valid access date and valid till date.

Procedure: dbo.EAlertQ_EnQueue_External
 Overall Workflow:
The stored procedure `[dbo].[EAlertQ_EnQueue_External]` enqueues an external email alert into the system. It receives input parameters for the sender, recipient, subject, attachment, and other details. The procedure inserts the alert details into the EAlertQ table, along with the created and updated timestamps, user ID, and active status. It then processes the SendTo, CC, and BCC fields by creating temporary tables, reading the ntext values, splitting them using a separator, and inserting the email addresses into their respective tables (EAlertQTo, EAlertQCC, and EAlertQBCC).

Input/Output Parameters:
- @From (nvarchar(250)): Sender's email address.
- @Sender (nvarchar(100)): Name of the sender.
- @Subject (nvarchar(500)): Subject of the email alert.
- @Sys (nvarchar(100)): System name or code.
- @Greetings (ntext): Greeting message for the recipient.
- @AlertMsg (ntext): Main content or body of the email alert.
- @UserId (nvarchar(50)): User ID who created and updated the alert.
- @SendTo (ntext): Recipient's email address, separated by a specific separator.
- @CC (ntext): Carbon copy recipients' email addresses, separated by a specific separator.
- @BCC (ntext): Blind carbon copy recipients' email addresses, separated by a specific separator.
- @Attachment (nvarchar(500)): File path of the attachment, if any.
- @Separator (nvarchar(1)): Specific separator used to split the SendTo, CC, and BCC fields.
- @AlertID (decimal(18, 0) output): Unique ID assigned to the alert after successful enqueue.

Tables Read/Written:
- EAlertQ: Stores the main alert details.
- EAlertQAtt: Stores the attachment details for the alert.
- EAlertQTo: Stores the recipients (SendTo) for the alert.
- EAlertQCC: Stores carbon copy recipients for the alert.
- EAlertQBCC: Stores blind carbon copy recipients for the alert. Temporary tables #tsendto, #tcc, and #tbcc are created during processing but dropped after use.

Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:
- If the alert ID is not zero, it means the insertion was successful, and the attachment is inserted into EAlertQAtt along with the alert ID.
- The procedure assumes that the separator between email addresses in the SendTo, CC, and BCC fields is a specific character (as specified by @Separator). If there are no email addresses or attachments, nothing will be inserted into the respective tables.

Procedure: dbo.EAlertQ_EnQueue
 Overall Workflow:
The stored procedure [dbo].[EAlertQ_EnQueue] is designed to enqueue an email alert. It takes input parameters such as sender, subject, system details, greetings, alert message, user ID, send-to, CC, BCC, and separator. The procedure inserts the alert into the EAlertQ table and then processes the recipients by splitting the send-to, CC, and BCC fields based on a specified separator. It creates temporary tables to store the split data, processes each recipient, and inserts them into their respective tables (EAlertQTo, EAlertQCC, or EAlertQBCC) before dropping the temporary tables.

- @CC (ntext, optional): CC recipients for the email alert.
- @BCC (ntext, optional): BCC recipients for the email alert.
- @Separator (nvarchar(1)): The separator used to split recipients' lists in SendTo, CC, and BCC parameters. Default is a comma.
- @AlertID (decimal(18, 0) output): The ID of the enqueued email alert.
- @From (nvarchar(250), optional): Email address to use as the sender if not provided in the input parameters.

- EAlertQ: The main table where the email alert is inserted.
- EAlertQTo, EAlertQCC, and EAlertQBCC: Tables containing the recipients for the email alert.

Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:
- If the SendTo parameter is null, the procedure returns without inserting any data.
- The status of the enqueued email alert is set to Q (Queued) by default, and its active status is set to 1.

- @AlertID (decimal(18, 0) output): Unique identifier assigned to each enqueued SMS alert
- @From (nvarchar(250) = null): Optional parameter for the sender's address if different from the one provided in the @Sender parameter

Tables Read/Written:
- SMSEAlertQ: Main table to store SMS alerts and their details
- SMSEAlertQTo: Table that stores recipients to whom the SMS alert is sent
- SMSEAlertQCC: Table that stores CC recipients for the SMS alert
- SMSEAlertQBCC: Table that stores BCC recipients for the SMS alert

Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:
- If @SendTo parameter is null, the procedure will exit without inserting any data.
- Status for each SMS alert in SMSEAlertQ table is defaulted to 'Q', and Active is defaulted to 1.
- The procedure processes each recipient, CC, and BCC by breaking them down into individual email addresses using a specified separator and stores them in their respective tables (SMSEAlertQTo, SMSEAlertQCC, or SMSEAlertQBCC).

Procedure: dbo.EAlertQ_EnQueue
 The provided SQL procedure, `dbo.EAlertQ_EnQueue`, is designed to enqueue emails for sending. Here's a summary of its workflow, inputs, outputs, tables read and written, and important business rules:

- **Overall Workflow**:
  1. Check if the `SendTo` parameter is not null before proceeding.
  2. Insert the email data into the `EAlertQ` table.
  3. Parse the `SendTo`, `CC`, and `BCC` parameters to separate individual recipients and insert them into the `EAlertQTo`, `EAlertQCC`, and `EAlertQBCC` tables, respectively.

- **Input Parameters**:
  - @Sender: The sender of the email.
  - @Subject: The subject of the email.
  - @Sys: The system name.
  - @Greetings: The greeting message for the email (ntext).
  - @AlertMsg: The main body of the alert message.
  - @UserId: The user ID creating and updating the record.
  - @SendTo, @CC, @BCC: Recipient lists separated by a specified separator.
  - @Separator: A separator character for parsing recipient lists.
  - @From (optional): The email address from which to send the message (defaults to null).
  - @AlertID (output): The unique identifier of the enqueued alert (decimal).

- **Output Parameters**:
  - @AlertID: The unique identifier of the enqueued alert.

- **Tables Read/Written**:
  - `EAlertQ`: Store the main email data.
  - `EAlertQTo`, `EAlertQCC`, and `EAlertQBCC`: Store recipient details for `SendTo`, `CC`, and `BCC`, respectively.

- **Important Conditional Logic/Business Rules**:
  - The status of the enqueued alert is set to 'Q' by default.
  - The active status of the enqueued alert is set to 1 by default.
  - If there are no recipients specified in the `SendTo`, `CC`, or `BCC` parameters, the procedure will return without doing anything.
  - If the recipient list contains multiple addresses, they will be inserted into their respective tables individually.
  - If a recipient list item is longer than half of the maximum `ntext` length (2^15 bytes), it will only be partially processed and stored in the tables.

Procedure: dbo.SMSEAlertQ_EnQueue
 **Procedure: SMSEAlertQ_EnQueue**

This is a stored procedure that enqueues an SMS alert for sending.

**Overall Workflow:**
1. Initializes a transaction.
2. Validates if the SendTo parameter is not null, and if so, proceeds.
3. Inserts the alert into SMSEAlertQ table with default status (Q) and active status (1).
4. Processes the SendTo parameter by breaking it down into individual recipients using a specified separator. Each recipient is then inserted into the SMSEAlertQTo table.
5. Repeats step 4 for CC and BCC parameters, inserting each email into the corresponding tables.
6. Commits the transaction upon successful execution of all steps.

**Input Parameters:**
- @Sender: Sender's name (nvarchar)
- @Subject: Subject of the alert (nvarchar)
- @Sys: System name (nvarchar)
- @Greetings: Greeting message for the alert (ntext)
- @AlertMsg: Main content of the alert (ntext)
- @UserId: User ID who created the alert (nvarchar)
- @SendTo: Recipients for the SMS alert (ntext)
- @CC: Carbon copy recipients for the SMS alert (ntext)
- @BCC: Blind carbon copy recipients for the SMS alert (ntext)
- @Separator: Separator used to split recipients in SendTo, CC, and BCC parameters (nvarchar)
- @From: Optional parameter specifying the sender's email address (nvarchar)
- @AlertID: Output parameter containing the ID of the inserted alert (decimal)

**Output Parameters:**
- @AlertID: The unique identifier for the newly created alert.

**Tables Read/Written:**
- SMSEAlertQ
- SMSEAlertQTo
- SMSEAlertQCC
- SMSEAlertQBCC

**Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:**
1. If the SendTo parameter is null, the procedure will return without inserting any records and not proceed further.
2. The default status for alerts is Q and the active status is 1.
3. Recipients in the SendTo, CC, and BCC parameters are processed by splitting the input using the specified separator character.

Procedure: dbo.SMTP_GET_Email_Lists
 Procedure Name: SMTP_GET_Email_Lists
Date Created: 16/03/2018
Purpose: Sends email alerts using SMTP

Workflow:
1. Sets the transaction isolation level to SERIALIZABLE
2. Deletes all records from EAlertQBCC, EAlertQCC, EAlertQTo, and EAlertQ where AlertMsg is NULL
3. Retrieves greetings, subject, alert message, sender, alert ID, system, CC recipients (using SMTP_GET_EMAIL_CC_LISTS), BCC recipients (using SMTP_GET_EMAIL_BCC_LISTS), and recipient email list for each active alert in the Q status from EALERTQ and EALERTQTO tables
4. Orders the results by ALERTID

1. Greetings
2. Subject
3. Alert Message
4. Sender
5. Alert ID
6. System
7. CC Recipient (using SMTP_GET_EMAIL_CC_LISTS)
8. BCC Recipient (using SMTP_GET_EMAIL_BCC_LISTS)
9. Recipient Email List

Tables Read/Written: EALERTQ, EALERTQTO, EAlertQBCC, EAlertQCC

Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:
1. Deletes all records with NULL AlertMsg
2. Only considers active alerts in the Q status
3. Constructs the recipient email list by concatenating all non-empty emails for a given alert ID from EALERTQTO table using XML PATH and FOR XML commands.

Procedure: dbo.sp_Generate_Ref_Num
 **Procedure: sp_Generate_Ref_Num**

- **Overall Workflow:** The procedure generates a reference number for a given form type, line, and track type. If the reference number does not exist for the specified parameters in the current year, it inserts a new record into the TAMS_RefSerialNumber table. Otherwise, it increments and updates the existing MaxNum.

  - `@Line`: A string representing the line (up to 20 characters).
  - `@TrackType`: A string representing the track type (up to 50 characters).

  - `@Message`: A message indicating any errors that occurred during the procedure execution.
