- **Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:**
  - If there are no records with the specified parameters in the TAMS_RefSerialNumber table for the current year, a new record is inserted.
  - If there is an existing record with the specified parameters in the TAMS_RefSerialNumber table for the current year, the MaxNum is incremented and updated.
  - For Depot track type, the line is appended with 'D'.
  - The generated reference number follows the format: `Line + '-' + FormType + '-' + Year(GETDATE()) + '-' + Right('00000' + Cast(@MaxNum as VARCHAR(5)), 5)`.

Procedure: dbo.sp_Generate_Ref_Num_TOA
 Procedure `sp_Generate_Ref_Num_TOA` is designed to generate reference numbers for specific forms and lines. Here's a summary of the workflow, input/output parameters, tables read/written, and important conditional logic or business rules.

- **Overall Workflow:**
  1. Initializes internal transaction and starts a new one if there is no active transaction.
  2. Calculates the operation date and current time as strings.
  3. Determines the reference number operation date and current time string based on the access date of the specified TAR ID.
  4. Checks if a reference number exists for the given form type, line, track type, year, and operation date. If not, inserts a new record; otherwise, increments the existing maximum number by 1.
  5. Generates the reference number based on the calculated values.
  6. Commits or rolls back the transaction depending on any errors encountered during the process.

- **Input/Output Parameters:**
  - `@FormType` (NVARCHAR(20)): The type of form for which the reference number is being generated.
  - `@Line` (NVARCHAR(20)): The line or department associated with the form.
  - `@TARID` (Int): The ID of the TAR record related to the access date.
  - `@OperationDate` (NVARCHAR(20)): The operation date for which the reference number is being generated.
  - `@TrackType` (NVARCHAR(50)): The type of track associated with the line (MainLine by default).
  - `@RefNum` (NVARCHAR(20) OUTPUT): The generated reference number.
  - `@Message` (NVARCHAR(500) OUTPUT): A message indicating any errors encountered during the process.

- **Tables Read/Written:**
  - TAMS_TAR: Contains TAR records with ID and access date.
  - TAMS_RefSerialNumber: Stores reference number serials for each form type, line, track type, year, and operation date.

- **Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:**
  - The procedure checks if a reference number already exists before generating a new one. If it does, the existing maximum number is incremented instead of creating a new record.
  - If the specified track type is 'Depot', the line value is appended with 'D' in the generated reference number.

Procedure: dbo.sp_Get_QRPoints
 **Procedure Overview:**
The SQL procedure `sp_Get_QRPoints` is designed to retrieve QR Code details from the `TAMS_TOA_QRCode` table in the `dbo` schema.

**Input/Output Parameters:**
This stored procedure does not take any input parameters and doesn't return any output parameters.

**Tables Read/Written:**
- `[dbo].[TAMS_TOA_QRCode]` (Table read)

**Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:**
The data is ordered by Line, Type, and Station, ensuring a specific order in the result set. The order by clause is `ORDER BY 2, 4, 3`, which translates to the Line, Type, and Station columns respectively.

Here's the SQL code for reference:
```sql
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[sp_Get_QRPoints]
AS
BEGIN
    SELECT [Sno], [Line], [Station], [Type], [URL], [QRCode]
      FROM [dbo].[TAMS_TOA_QRCode]
      ORDER BY 2, 4, 3
END
GO
```

Procedure: dbo.SP_SMTP_Send_SMSAlert
 **Procedure Overview:**

The SQL procedure, `[dbo].[SP_SMTP_Send_SMSAlert]`, is designed to send SMS alerts using the SMTP method.

**Input Parameters:**
- @p_Alertid (integer)
- @p_from (varchar)
- @p_To (varchar)
- @p_Alertmsg (varchar(max))
- @p_sysname (varchar(50))

**Output Parameters:**
No explicit output parameters are defined in this procedure. However, it updates the `SMSEAlertQ` table with a new status and timestamps.

**Tables Read/Written:**
- dbo.SMSEAlertQ (reads to fetch alerts and update their status)
- dbo.SMSEAlertQTo (reads to fetch recipients for each alert)
- Uses the `[dbo].[SP_SMTP_SMS_NetPage]` stored procedure internally

**Conditional Logic/Business Rules:**
- The procedure uses two cursors, `@CurMain` and `@CurDetl`, to iterate through alerts and their recipients respectively.
- Alerts are fetched from the `SMSEAlertQ` table with a status of 'Q'.
- Recipients for each alert are fetched from the `SMSEAlertQTo` table, where the `AlertID` matches the current alert.
- For each recipient, the `[dbo].[SP_SMTP_SMS_NetPage]` stored procedure is called to send the SMS alert.
- After sending an alert to all its recipients, the status of the alert in the `SMSEAlertQ` table is updated to 'S', and the current date and username are stored as `LastUpdatedOn` and `LastUpdatedBy` respectively.
- The procedure continues fetching alerts and sending them until there are no more alerts with a status of 'Q'.

Procedure: dbo.SP_SMTP_SMS_NetPage
 The SQL procedure `SP_SMTP_SMS_NetPage` is designed to send SMS alerts using the NetPage application.

- **Overall Workflow**: The procedure first deletes old records from the `SMTP_SMSAlertQ` table that are more than 60 days old. Then, it inserts a new record into the same table with the provided parameters (from, to, alert message ID, actual message, system name, created date, and created by). After that, it executes an xp_cmdshell command to send the SMS using the NetPage application.

- **Input Parameters**: The procedure takes five input parameters: `@From` (the sender's number), `@To` (the recipient's mobile number), `@ActualMsg` (the actual SMS message content), `@AlertiD` (alert ID), and `@SysName` (system name).

- **Output Parameters**: The procedure doesn't explicitly return any output parameters. However, it does insert a record into the `SMTP_SMSAlertQ` table and implicitly returns its identity (the ID of the newly inserted record). It also raises an error message if there's an issue while creating the log table.

- **Tables Read/Written**: The procedure reads from and writes to the `SMTP_SMSAlertQ` table.

- **Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules**: If there's an error while creating the log table, the procedure raises an error message and stops execution. Additionally, it only sends SMS alerts for records that are less than 60 days old in the `SMTP_SMSAlertQ` table (due to the deletion of old records at the beginning of the procedure).

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Applicant_List_Child_OnLoad
 **Procedure Overview:**
The provided SQL script is a stored procedure named `sp_TAMS_Applicant_List_Child_OnLoad`. This procedure retrieves and organizes the applicant list data based on certain parameters.

**Input Parameters:**
- @Line: Represents the line of the sector (e.g., 'DTL', 'NEL').
- @TrackType: Unspecified filter for Track Type.
- @ToAccessDate and @FromAccessDate: Specify the range of access dates.
- @TARType: Filter for TAR type.
- @SectorID: The ID of the sector to focus on.

**Output Parameters:**
This procedure does not return any output parameters explicitly, but it generates a result set with applicant list details when executed.

**Tables Read/Written:**
- TAMS_TAR: Applicant Tracking Application table
- TAMS_TAR_Sector: Links between TAMS_TAR and sector tables
- TAMS_WFStatus: Workflow statuses for applicants
- TAMS_Sector: Sector details
- A temporary table #TmpAppList is created to store the filtered data during the process.

**Important Conditional Logic/Business Rules:**
- The procedure filters the data based on the provided parameters, such as line, sector ID, track type, access dates, and TAR type.
- Only active sectors are considered.
- If the direction of the sector is 'BB' or 'NB', it will be assigned a direction value of 1; otherwise, it will receive a direction value of 2.
- The applicant data is filtered by the access dates and TAR type provided or optional parameters.
- The result set displays the applicant list organized by TARID with specified fields: TARNo, TARType, AccessDate, AccessType, Company, WFStatus, ColorCode, and Sector information based on the chosen sector ID.
- At the end of the procedure, the temporary table #TmpAppList is dropped.

 Workflow:
1. The stored procedure `sp_TAMS_Applicant_List_Child_OnLoad_20220303` is created to retrieve a list of applicants based on provided parameters.
2. It first initializes variables and creates temporary tables #TmpSector and #TmpAppList for storing sector data and applicant data, respectively.
3. The temporary tables are truncated before inserting new data.
4. Sector data is inserted into the #TmpSector table based on the provided `Line` parameter, effective date range, and active status.
5. Applicant data is then inserted into the #TmpAppList table based on matching TAR, sector, workflow status, line, active status, access date range, TAR type, and sector direction.
6. The final output is generated by selecting applicant data from the #TmpAppList table where the `SectorID` matches the provided parameter.
7. Finally, the temporary tables are dropped.

- @ToAccessDate: To access date in YYYY-MM-DD format (NVARCHAR(20)) - Not used directly but utilized to convert dates
- @FromAccessDate: From access date in YYYY-MM-DD format (NVARCHAR(20)) - Not used directly but utilized to convert dates

- TAMS_TAR: Read to get applicant data
- TAMS_WFStatus: Read to get workflow status data
- #TmpSector: Created and written to store sector data temporarily
- #TmpAppList: Created and written to store applicant data temporarily

Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:
1. The procedure checks if the provided `Line` parameter is active and within the effective date range.
2. The procedure filters applicants based on the access date, TAR type, and sector direction. If no TAR type is provided, it accepts all TAR types.
3. The direction of each sector is used to sort the sectors and applicants in ascending or descending order. Sectors with directions 'BB' (Bottom-to-Top) or 'NB' (North-to-South) are sorted accordingly.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Applicant_List_OnLoad
 Title: Procedure for Loading Applicant List Based on Input Parameters

Overall Workflow:
- The stored procedure `sp_TAMS_Applicant_List_OnLoad` accepts four input parameters and generates a list of applicants based on the given line, access date range, TAR type, and sector.
- It first truncates two temporary tables (#TmpSector and #TmpAppList) for fresh data.
- Then, it populates the #TmpSector table with sector details based on the provided line, active status, effective date, and expiry date.
- Next, it fills the #TmpAppList table with applicant information, joining multiple tables (TAMS_TAR, TAMS_TAR_Sector, TAMS_WFStatus, TAMS_Sector) based on specific conditions. These conditions include the line, track type, workflow status, sector ID, and access date range.
- After that, it sorts the applicant list in ascending and descending order according to the sector order for sectors with directions 'BB' or 'NB'.
- Finally, it joins the #TmpSector and #TmpAppList tables to generate the final output, and drops both temporary tables.

Input Parameters:
- @Line (NVARCHAR(10)) - Line associated with the applicant list.
- @ToAccessDate (NVARCHAR(20)) - To access date for filtering applicants.
- @FromAccessDate (NVARCHAR(20)) - From access date for filtering applicants.
- @TARType (NVARCHAR(20)) - Type of TAR associated with the applicant list.

Output Parameters:
- The procedure does not have any output parameters.

Tables Read/Written:
- Read: TAMS_Sector, TAMS_TAR, TAMS_TAR_Sector, TAMS_WFStatus
- Written: #TmpSector, #TmpAppList (temporary tables)

Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:
- The procedure checks if the provided line, track type, sector, and date ranges are valid based on active status and effective/expiry dates.
- It also handles the direction of sectors ('BB' or 'NB') by sorting applicants accordingly in ascending and descending order.
- If there is no match for a provided line and track type, the final output will be empty.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Approval_Del_BufferZone
 Procedure `sp_TAMS_Approval_Del_BufferZone` is a stored procedure in the `dbo` schema. It takes three parameters: `@TARID` (a BIGINT, default value 0), `@SectorID` (also a BIGINT, default value 0), and `@Message` (an NVARCHAR with a maximum length of 500 and a default value NULL OUTPUT).

The overall workflow is as follows:
1. Initialize internal transaction variable `@IntrnlTrans` to 0.
2. If there are no ongoing transactions, start a new one by setting `@IntrnlTrans` to 1 and beginning the transaction.
3. Delete records from the `TAMS_TAR_Sector` table where `TARId` matches `@TARID` and `SectorId` matches `@SectorID`.
4. If an error occurs during the delete operation, set the output parameter `@Message` to 'ERROR INSERTING INTO TAMS_TAR' and jump to the `TRAP_ERROR` label. Otherwise, continue with the rest of the procedure.
5. Execute the `FORCE_EXIT_PROC` label if the internal transaction is active, committing the transaction. The procedure then returns the output parameter `@Message`.
6. If an error occurs during the execution of the procedure and the internal transaction is active, jump to the `TRAP_ERROR` label, rollback the transaction, and return the output parameter `@Message`.
7. The `TRAP_ERROR` label is used for error handling.

The stored procedure reads from and writes to the `TAMS_TAR_Sector` table. It does not appear to contain any conditional logic or business rules beyond the delete operation, as the provided code only shows the deletion of records.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Approval_Endorse_20220930
 Procedure: `sp_TAMS_Approval_Endorse_20220930` is a SQL stored procedure that handles the approval and endorsement process of TAR forms.

**Overall Workflow:**
1. The stored procedure takes input parameters such as TAR ID, current WF ID, current Endorser ID, current Endorser Level, remarks, TVF Run Mode, TVF Run Mode Update Indicator, User Login ID, and outputs a message.
2. It first checks if there is no ongoing transaction (`@@TRANCOUNT = 0`) and begins a new one if necessary.
3. It updates the TAR Workflow status to 'Approved', sets the action by and action on fields, and optionally updates the TVF Run Mode based on the `TVFRunModeUpdInd` parameter.
4. The procedure then determines whether it's the last level of approval or if there is a next level endorser.
   - If it's the last level, it sets the TAR status accordingly and sends an email if necessary (for late forms).
   - If there's a next level endorser, it inserts a new workflow record for the next endorser and updates the TAR status. If it's a late form, it sends an email alert to the next role.
5. The stored procedure logs the approval action and handles any errors that may occur during execution.

**Input Parameters:**
- `@TARID`: TAR ID
- `@TARWFID`: Current WF ID
- `@EID`: Current Endorser ID
- `@ELevel`: Current Endorser Level
- `@Remarks`: Remarks (mandatory for reject, optional for approved/endorse)
- `@TVFRunMode`: New column to be confirmed with Adeline
- `@TVFRunModeUpdInd`: Indicator to update TVF Run Mode or not.
- `@UserLI`: User Login ID
- `@Message`: Output message (set to empty at the start)

**Output Parameters:**
- `@Message`: Contains an error message if there's an error during execution.

**Tables Read/Written:**
1. Tables read: TAMS_User, TAMS_TAR_Workflow, TAMS_TAR, TAMS_Endorser, TAMS_Action_Log, and TAMS_Workflow.
2. Tables written: TAMS_TAR_Workflow, TAMS_TAR (if last level), and TAMS_Action_Log.

**Important Conditional Logic or Business Rules:**
- The stored procedure checks if the current endorser's level is the last level of approval or if there's a next level endorser.
- If it's the last level, it sets the TAR status to 9 (for NEL) or 8 (for DTL/LRT).
- The stored procedure sends emails based on certain conditions such as late forms and the next role alert.
- It also logs approval actions in the action log table.
- If the workflow type is 'LateAfter' and involve power is 1, it sends an email to the OCC role if the current endorser level is 2.

 Title: Procedure for TAMS Approval and Endorse (2023-04-10)

- TAMS_Workflow

2. Checking for conflicts in sector assignments (i.e., ensuring that no two access requests overlap in terms of time and location).

3. Determining exceptions based on the requirement of validation for current level endorsers.

4. Retrieving additional information related to power requirements for track access.

Here's a brief overview of the main sections:

1. The first part defines the parameters for the stored procedure, `@Line` and `@TrackType`. These parameters are used to filter data based on line number and track type.

2. The second part consists of multiple SQL statements that retrieve data from various tables, including track status, endorser information, sector assignments, and access requirements.

* Sends an email to the endorser (if applicable) for approval or rejection.
* Updates the TAR's status if the next level endorser does not exist.

Procedure: dbo.sp_TAMS_Approval_Endorse_20220930
Here's a concise summary of the provided stored procedure in bulleted points:

* It takes several input parameters, including TAR ID, current workflow ID, endorser ID, level, remarks, and user login ID.

**Input/Output Parameters**

* Input:
	+ `@TARID` (INTEGER): TAR ID
	+ `@TARWFID` (INTEGER): Current workflow ID
	+ `@EID` (INTEGER): Current endorser ID
	+ `@ELevel` (INTEGER): Current endorser level
	+ `@Remarks` (NVARCHAR(1000)): Remarks for approval/rejection/endorsement
	+ `@TVFRunMode` (NVARCHAR(50)): New column to be confirmed with Adeline
	+ `@TVFRunModeUpdInd` (NVARCHAR(5)): Indicator to update TVF run mode or not
	+ `@UserLI` (NVARCHAR(50)): User login ID
* Output:
	+ `@Message` (NVARCHAR(500)): Error message if any

	+ TAMS_User
	+ TAMS_TAR_Workflow
	+ TAMS_Endorser
	+ TAMS_TAR
	+ TAMS_Action_Log

	+ TAMS_TAR_Workflow (insert/update)
	+ TAMS_TAR (update)

**Conditional Logic/Business Rules**

* If the TVF run mode needs to be updated, it updates the TAR status ID and the TAR status date.
* If the next level endorser exists, it inserts a new workflow entry with the next level endorser's details or updates the TAR status ID if no next level endorser exists.
* If the TAR type is 'Late', it sends an email to the role IDs involved in the process.
* It also triggers an action log entry for the approved TAR form.
* Depending on the workflow type and involvement power, it may send additional emails or perform other actions.
